creations-chat 2022-12-06 14:17:03 well, uncool things about roscale is that they're too simplified and sometimes people intend to stick with some 'formula' with the bones of the build. summarizing motorlocks as simple as possible but keeping detail in an impossible level of grade (same with functions) is the key of making a good roscale build. try to make more things and always keep away from the solid principles, it's necessary to get experience from failure such as miscalculation of space, wrong proportions, or some malfunctioning mechanics.
in your current build just push the intake shadow block backwards or paint the motor black to give some depth and adjust canopy angels with piston lock in order to make smooth curves. i recommend you TNT locking to avoid bugs, jammed springs, disconnector parts sticking outside.
